function info($str) { echo "INFO: $str\n"; }
function warn($str) { echo "WARNING: $str\n"; }
function err($str) { die("FATAL ERROR: $str\n"); }

@set_time_limit(0);

@header('Content-Type: text/plain');

chdir(__DIR__);
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 433') {
	err('This update can only be applied to OIDplus version 2.0.0.433!');
}

if (version_compare(PHP_VERSION, '7.0.0') < 0) {
	err('You need PHP Version 7.0 to update to this version');
}

if (!is_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
	writefile_1();
	if (!is_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
	} else if (sha1_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt') != '3f2757d3f0b6fe0a9f970eba38954d25c6de3e72') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt') !== '3f2757d3f0b6fe0a9f970eba38954d25c6de3e72') {
		if (@sha1_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt') !== 'bfa0980287013c5ab97949d88d26dc80809a46bf') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
			$tmp = pathinfo('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_1();
		if (@sha1_file('doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt') !== '3f2757d3f0b6fe0a9f970eba38954d25c6de3e72') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): doc/google_oauth2_installation.txt');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('index.php')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: index.php');
	writefile_2();
	if (!is_file('index.php')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): index.php');
	} else if (sha1_file('index.php') != '97d1112d21f649a8f36449bf92938563e64145ae') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): index.php');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('index.php', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of index.php');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '97d1112d21f649a8f36449bf92938563e64145ae') {
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== 'c659dc04d651a8f1bf769cc13bb4a1484a017b8f') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: index.php');
			$tmp = pathinfo('index.php');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('index.php')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('index.php', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_2();
		if (@sha1_file('index.php') !== '97d1112d21f649a8f36449bf92938563e64145ae') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): index.php');
		}
	}
}

			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_4();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html') !== 'a46b0f213d49eee7abe15c0b1027617a155db56b') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation$dede.html');
		}
	}
}

if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
	warn('File has vanished! Will re-create it: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	writefile_5();
	if (!is_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')) {
		warn('File cannot be created (not existing): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if (sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') != 'f4a45d9a20cbe87080fabc3f64cba0eddc0dff6a') {
		warn('File cannot be created (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	} else if ((DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR === '/') && !@chmod('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', 0644)) {
		warn('Could not change file permissions of res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
	}
} else {
	if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f4a45d9a20cbe87080fabc3f64cba0eddc0dff6a') {
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'b194bcfac1eb84dd1d6b75f10fe6e97c7d850dec') {
			warn('File was modified. Will overwrite the changes now: res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$tmp = pathinfo('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
			$backup_name = $tmp['dirname'].DIRECTORY_SEPARATOR.$tmp['filename'].'.'.date('Ymdhis',@filemtime('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html')).(isset($tmp['extension']) ? '.'.$tmp['extension'] : '');
			warn('Creating a backup as '.$backup_name);
			if (!@copy('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html', $backup_name)) {
				warn('Creation of backup failed');
			}
		}
		writefile_5();
		if (@sha1_file('res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html') !== 'f4a45d9a20cbe87080fabc3f64cba0eddc0dff6a') {
			warn('File cannot be written (checksum mismatch): res/OIDplus/privacy_documentation.html');
		}
	}
}


file_put_contents('oidplus_version.txt', "Revision 434\n");
if (trim(@file_get_contents('oidplus_version.txt')) !== 'Revision 434') err('Could not write to oidplus_version.txt!');


echo 'DONE'; // This exact string will be compared in Update v3

@unlink(__FILE__);
if (is_file(__FILE__)) warn('Could not delete '.basename(__FILE__).'! Please delete it manually');
